# STATE Archive — `aDNA.aDNA/STATE.md` Historical Sessions

> Immortal-spine for `aDNA.aDNA` STATE.md history. Sections move here when superseded in the router. The router is `aDNA.aDNA/STATE.md`. This file is **append-only by convention**: new sections land at the top under a date header; existing sections never get edited (per project Standing Order #6 — archive, never delete).

> **Origin**: Initial split from monolithic `aDNA.aDNA/STATE.md` (598 lines / 351,783 bytes / ~88 kT content-load) at M2.1 S2 2026-05-19. Pre-split SHA `1e337db`. Design at [[how/campaigns/campaign_adna_serious_tool_readiness/missions/artifacts/m21_obj2_state_split_design.md|m21_obj2_state_split_design.md]]. Convention at [[how/campaigns/campaign_adna_serious_tool_readiness/missions/artifacts/m21_obj4_archive_convention_design.md|m21_obj4_archive_convention_design.md]].

> **Note on line 374 marker + line 378 body pairing**: the `## Last Session DEPRECATED-marker — campaign_adna_serious_tool_readiness P0 OPENED 2026-05-17` header at original line 374 is the deprecation marker for the `## Last Session (2026-05-17 — campaign_adna_serious_tool_readiness OPENED ...)` block that immediately follows (originally lines 378+). Both move here as a paired unit. The non-marker header form is preserved verbatim.

(B3) Smoke `bash .adna/how/standard/hooks/pre-push-sanitize.sh --self-test` → **PASSED 7/7** (2 clean CLEAN + 5 dirty flagged by named rule each); exit 0. **2 in-session defect fixes (BONUS — both surfaced by verification)**: **(Defect 1) Skill path mismatch** — 4 v7.0 skill files (skill_deploy.md, skill_vault_publish.md, skill_publish_tarball.md, plus hook header) referenced `.adna/how/standard/hooks/pre-push-sanitize.sh` (pre-M03-flatten path, when vaults had child `.adna/` template subdir). Post-flatten reality (per `skill_project_fork.md` line 84-90 + `aDNA.aDNA/CLAUDE.md` Standing Rule 1): vaults are SIBLINGS of `.adna/` and contain COPY of template content as vault-local — no child `.adna/`. Rewrite spec line 312 explicitly anticipates BOTH paths ("template-shipped" vs "inherits/customizes locally") but S1 implementation only checked one, so A3 would've failed at Step 1. Fix: change all 4 files to check `how/standard/hooks/pre-push-sanitize.sh` FIRST (canonical post-flatten), fallback to `.adna/how/standard/hooks/pre-push-sanitize.sh` (legacy). Hook header comment also updated to name both source locations. **(Defect 2) R2 secret-pattern quote-class bug** — all 7 patterns in `secret_patterns` used `[\x27\x22]?` to mean "optional single or double quote". POSIX `grep -E` does NOT interpret `\xNN` as hex escapes (that's PCRE territory). With legacy `'...'` quoting, the patterns contained 8 LITERAL characters `\`, `x`, `2`, `7`, `\`, `x`, `2`, `2` — never matching `'` or `"`, silently missing every QUOTED secret in production push-time R2 scans. Surfaced when self-test against quoted-secret fixture failed. Fix: switch all 7 patterns from `'...'` to bash ANSI-C quoting `$'...'` (which DOES expand `\x27`/`\x22` to `'`/`"`); preserves `\-` via `\\-` to keep regex semantics intact. Verified: same patterns now match the quoted AWS-style fixture; push-time R2 path uses the same shared `secret_patterns` array so fix propagates. **Files modified**: `.adna/how/skills/skill_deploy.md` + `.adna/how/skills/skill_vault_publish.md` + `.adna/how/skills/skill_publish_tarball.md` + `.adna/how/standard/hooks/pre-push-sanitize.sh` (header + self-test + secret_patterns) + `.adna/how/standard/hooks/test_fixtures/` (8 new files). **Files created in aDNA.aDNA**: `how/sessions/active/session_stanley_20260518_054924_adna_v2_m05_s2.md` (session file; moves to history at close); M05 mission file `## Session log` block updated with S2 entry. **M05 stays `in_progress`** — S3 = AAR authoring (lightweight 5-line + extended findings appendix per M01/M03/M04/M08a precedent; load-bearing finding candidates: skill-path mismatch defect class + R2 quote-class defect class + verification-as-first-class M05 deliverable) + status flips (M05 → completed; M06 → next; campaign master amendments entry; STATE.md rewrite) + **v8 M1.1 coord checkpoint fires at M05 close** (notify in `campaign_adna_serious_tool_readiness`) + Daedalus/Spacemacs migration Steps 1-4 announcement memo.
